    "windows_role": "sensors",
    "meta_domain_role": "shared relational space",
    "channels_role": "ratios within meta-domain"
  },

  "meta_domain_definition": {
    "name": "window_motion_state",
    "components": [
      "magnitude",
      "direction",
      "coherence",
      "rate",
      "stability"
    ],
    "constraint": "all components must be dimensionless and comparable across windows"
  },

  "code_changes": [
    {
      "action": "add_function",
      "name": "compute_motion_state",
      "code": "def compute_motion_state(current, prev, history, eps=1e-12):\n    \"\"\"\n    Convert raw window values into a dimensionless motion-state.\n    current: [W1, W2, W3]\n    prev: previous values\n    history: dict with rolling history lists for each domain\n    \"\"\"\n    if prev is None:\n        return np.zeros(3), np.zeros(3)\n\n    delta = current - prev\n\n    # magnitude normalized by local history\n    mag = np.zeros(3)\n    for i, key in enumerate(['W1', 'W2', 'W3']):\n        hist = history[key]\n        scale = np.mean(hist) + eps if len(hist) > 0 else eps\n        mag[i] = abs(delta[i]) / scale\n\n    # direction (sign only)\n    direction = np.sign(delta)\n\n    return mag, direction\n"
    },

    {
      "action": "add_function",
      "name": "compute_meta_vector",
      "code": "def compute_meta_vector(mag, direction, eps=1e-12):\n    \"\"\"\n    Combine magnitude and direction into a unified meta-domain vector.\n    \"\"\"\n    # normalize magnitude vector\n    mag_norm = mag / (np.sum(mag) + eps)\n\n    # embed direction as weighting\n    meta = mag_norm * (direction + 1.0) / 2.0\n\n    return meta\n"
    },

    {
      "action": "replace_global_shell_input",
      "details": [
        "Remove direct use of W1/W2/W3 or their raw deltas.",

        "Use meta-domain shell values instead of raw or delta W values."

    },

    {
      "action": "add_history_tracking",
      "details": [
        "Maintain rolling history for each domain for normalization."
      ],
      "code": "history = {'W1': [], 'W2': [], 'W3': []}\n\n# update history each frame\nfor i, key in enumerate(['W1', 'W2', 'W3']):\n    history[key].append(abs(delta[i]))\n    if len(history[key]) > 100:\n        history[key].pop(0)\n"
    },

{
  "agent_task": "rigorous_groove_learning_validation_v1",
  "goal": "Distinguish true trajectory-specific groove learning from smoothing, momentum, or routing artifacts.",

  "core_hypothesis": {
    "claim": "The platform learns wave trajectories by deepening identity-specific continuation grooves.",
    "must_show": [
      "same trajectory becomes easier to continue",
      "different trajectories do not benefit from the wrong groove",
      "previously learned grooves survive later training",
      "groove helps when external input is partially removed",
      "noise does not falsely create strong grooves"
    ]
  },

  "test_battery": [
    {
      "id": "T1_repeated_A_learning_curve",
      "purpose": "Prove groove deepening across repeated traversal.",
      "sequence": [
        "clear_memory",
        "A_pass1",
        "A_pass2",
        "A_pass3",
        "A_pass4",
        "A_pass5",
        "replay_A"
      ],
      "success": [
        "same groove_id dominates across A passes",
        "continuation_mismatch_mean trend decreases",
        "replay_A < A_pass1",
        "trace_feedback_gain or successful_traversals increases"
      ]
    },
    {
      "id": "T2_A_vs_B_directionality",
      "purpose": "Prove groove is directional, not generic smoothing.",
      "sequence": [
        "train_A_5_passes",
        "run_B_without_training",
        "run_A_again"
      ],
      "success": [
        "B mismatch > trained_A mismatch",
        "B routes to different groove or fails to lock to A groove",
        "A_after_B returns to A groove",
        "A_after_B mismatch remains near trained_A mismatch"
      ]
    },
    {
      "id": "T3_catastrophic_forgetting",
      "purpose": "Test whether training B damages learned A.",
      "sequence": [
        "clear_memory",
        "train_A_5_passes",
        "record_A_metrics",
        "train_B_5_passes",
        "replay_A",
        "replay_B"
      ],
      "success": [
        "replay_A uses original A groove",
        "replay_A mismatch does not degrade more than 10-15%",
        "replay_B uses B groove",
        "A and B groove_ids remain distinct"
      ]
    },
    {
      "id": "T4_withheld_continuation",
      "purpose": "Test continuation when external wave is reduced or removed.",
      "sequence": [
        "train_A_5_passes",
        "run_A_with_last_40_percent_zeroed_or_masked",

      ],
      "success": [
        "internal continuation remains aligned for a measurable horizon",
        "continuation_mismatch rises gradually, not immediately",
        "trained_A continuation beats untrained baseline"
      ]
    },
    {
      "id": "T5_noise_floor_control",
      "purpose": "Prevent false learning from noise.",
      "sequence": [
        "clear_memory",
        "run_white_noise",
        "run_pink_noise",
        "run_A_after_noise",
        "train_A_3_passes"
      ],
      "success": [
        "noise does not create stable high-confidence groove",
        "A still forms its own groove",
        "noise groove, if created, has low success_count",
        "adaptive threshold rejects unstable trace segments"
      ]
    },
    {
      "id": "T6_transition_warning",
      "purpose": "Test undesired-event detection as loss of continuation alignment.",
      "sequence": [
        "train_A_5_passes",
        "run_A_to_transition_wave",
        "measure mismatch before transition boundary"
      ],
      "success": [
        "continuation_mismatch rises before or at transition",
        "groove_id instability increases near transition",
        "operator sequence changes before event segment dominates"
      ]
    }
  ],

  "metrics_required": [

{
  "patch_name": "v14_stage2_add_diffusion",
  "purpose": "Add native family-space diffusion to v14 so bands emerge from the signature field instead of being inferred only from peak expansion.",
  "applies_to": {
    "surface": "v14",
    "baseline": "v14 Stage 1",
    "rationale": [
      "Stage 1 already has signature-native state, peak+band detection, dynamic corridor gating, orientation operators, reasoning loop, and binary readout.",
      "The current conceptual update uses retention, gated writeback, and boundary penalty, but diffusion is not yet integrated as a first-class term."
    ],
    "citations": [
      ":contentReference[oaicite:0]{index=0}"
    ]
  },
  "core_change": {
    "old_update_rule": "signature_next = (1 - lambda) * signature_current + kappa * gated_delta - eta * boundary_penalty",
    "new_update_rule": "signature_next = (1 - lambda) * signature_current + kappa * gated_delta + D_f * Laplacian_family(signature_current) - eta * boundary_penalty",
    "optional_extended_rule": "signature_next = (1 - lambda) * signature_current + kappa * gated_delta + D_f * Laplacian_family(signature_current) + D_o * Laplacian_orientation(signature_current) - eta * boundary_penalty",
    "term_meaning": {
      "lambda": "overwrite permeability / relaxation",
      "kappa": "write gain",
      "D_f": "family-space diffusion coefficient",
      "D_o": "optional orientation-channel diffusion coefficient",
      "eta": "boundary / corridor penalty"
    }
  },
  "files_to_add": [
    {
      "path": "v14/core/diffusion_ops.py",
      "responsibility": [
        "implement 1D family-lattice Laplacian",
        "implement optional orientation diffusion",
        "support wraparound and non-wrap boundary modes",
        "return diffusion diagnostics for trace/reporting"
      ]
    }
  ],
  "files_to_modify": [
    {
      "path": "v14/core/signature_state.py",
      "changes": [
        "store diffusion coefficients in state/config access",

        "optionally expose diffusion_mass or spread summary"
      ]
    },

        "use diffused amplitude for subsequent peak/band detection"
      ]
    },
    {
      "path": "v14/core/peak_detector.py",

      ]
    },

    {
      "path": "v14/config/config_v14_scaffold.json",
      "changes": [
        "add family_diffusion",
        "add orientation_diffusion",
        "add diffusion_boundary_mode",
        "add use_wraparound_lattice"
      ]
    }
  ],
  "new_config_fields": {
    "family_diffusion": {
      "type": "float",
      "default": 0.12,
      "range_hint": [0.0, 0.5],
      "meaning": "local redistribution across neighboring family slots"
    },
    "orientation_diffusion": {
      "type": "float",
      "default": 0.0,
      "range_hint": [0.0, 0.25],
      "meaning": "optional redistribution across orientation channels"
    },
    "diffusion_boundary_mode": {
      "type": "string",
      "default": "wrap",
      "allowed": ["wrap", "reflect", "clamp"],
      "meaning": "how diffusion behaves at lattice boundaries"
    },
    "use_wraparound_lattice": {
      "type": "boolean",
      "default": true,
      "meaning": "treat family lattice as cyclic"
    }
  },
  "minimal_diffusion_ops_py": {
    "module_name": "diffusion_ops.py",
    "code_outline": [
      "import numpy as np",
      "",
      "def laplacian_family_1d(arr, mode='wrap'):",
      "    arr = np.asarray(arr, dtype=float)",
      "    if mode == 'wrap':",
      "        left = np.roll(arr, 1)",
      "        right = np.roll(arr, -1)",
      "    elif mode == 'reflect':",
      "        left = np.empty_like(arr); right = np.empty_like(arr)",
      "        left[1:] = arr[:-1]; left[0] = arr[1]",
      "        right[:-1] = arr[1:]; right[-1] = arr[-2]",
      "    elif mode == 'clamp':",
      "        left = np.empty_like(arr); right = np.empty_like(arr)",
      "        left[1:] = arr[:-1]; left[0] = arr[0]",
      "        right[:-1] = arr[1:]; right[-1] = arr[-1]",
      "    else:",
      "        raise ValueError(f'Unknown diffusion boundary mode: {mode}')",
      "    return left + right - 2.0 * arr",
      "",
      "def apply_family_diffusion(arr, coeff, mode='wrap'):",
      "    lap = laplacian_family_1d(arr, mode=mode)",
      "    diff = coeff * lap",
      "    return arr + diff, diff, lap"
    ]
  },
  "reasoning_loop_insertion": {
    "current_phase_order": [
      "read",
      "score",
      "choose",
      "gate",
      "writeback",
      "stability/phase updates",
      "trace"
    ],
    "new_phase_order": [
      "read",
      "score",
      "choose",
      "gate",
      "writeback",
      "diffuse",
      "stability/phase updates",
      "peak_and_band_refresh",
      "trace"
    ],
    "pseudocode": [
      "gated_delta = ...",
      "pre_diff_amplitude = state.signature.amplitude.copy()",
      "written = (1 - lambda) * pre_diff_amplitude + kappa * gated_delta - eta * boundary_penalty",
      "post_diff_amplitude, diff_term, lap = apply_family_diffusion(written, family_diffusion, mode=diffusion_boundary_mode)",
      "state.signature.amplitude = clip_or_normalize(post_diff_amplitude)",
      "peaks, bands = detect_peaks_and_bands(state.signature.amplitude, ...)"
    ]
  },
  "peak_and_band_revision": {
    "old_behavior": "bands are expanded heuristically from peaks",
    "new_behavior": "bands are contiguous regions of support in the diffused amplitude field above threshold, optionally anchored to nearby peaks",
    "implementation_notes": [
      "detect peaks first",
      "find contiguous indices above band threshold",
      "associate each band with its nearest/strongest peak",
      "support wraparound merging when use_wraparound_lattice is true"
    ]
  },
  "corridor_revision": {
    "old_behavior": "corridor window derived mainly from peaks and simple band expansion",
    "new_behavior": "corridor window derived from diffused band width and support mass",
    "example_rule": {
      "window_width_i": "base_width + alpha * local_band_width + beta * local_diffusion_mass",
      "entry_resistance_i": "base_entry / (1 + gamma * local_band_support)",
      "exit_resistance_i": "base_exit * (1 + delta * local_stability)"
    }
  },
  "trace_additions": {
    "phase_trace_fields": {
      "diffusion_energy": "sum(abs(diff_term))",
      "spread_measure": "sum(abs(laplacian))",
      "band_widths_after": "list of widths of detected bands after diffusion",
      "top_peaks_before": "already present / keep",
      "top_peaks_after": "already present / keep"
    }
  },
  "report_additions": {
    "fields": [
      "family_diffusion",
      "diffusion_energy_mean",
      "diffusion_energy_max",
      "spread_measure_mean",
      "mean_band_width",
      "max_band_width"
    ],
    "goal": "show whether diffusion is actually shaping topology rather than being numerically inert"
  },
  "initial_tuning_profiles": {
    "diffusion_low": {
      "family_diffusion": 0.05,
      "expected_behavior": "slight smoothing, minimal band growth"
    },
    "diffusion_mid": {
      "family_diffusion": 0.12,
      "expected_behavior": "visible band formation, better corridor stability"
    },
    "diffusion_high": {

    }

  "acceptance_checks": [

  "non_goals_for_this_patch": [

{
  "spec_name": "v15_projection_admissibility_architecture",
  "status": "proposed",
  "intent": "Fold the v14 engine, the additive DAAS path, the practical-vs-objective distinction, and the new projection-controlled visual model into one forward spec.",
  "core_claim": "v15 begins when the organizing center shifts from response stabilization to admissible projection.",
  "one_sentence_definition": "v15 is a projection-governed reasoning architecture in which full structure remains primary, usable output is a conditioned extraction, and no readout is allowed unless its projection path is structurally admissible.",
  "why_v15_exists": {
    "problem_statement": [
      "Current LLM-like systems often produce practical coherence without full structural validation.",
      "v14 already improves this through corridor gating, caution, hold, recovery, trace, residue, and state export, but its center of gravity is still stabilization plus readout.",
      "The next step is not a cosmetic redesign, but a structural shift: projection legitimacy must become the first-class object."
    ],
    "target_failure_to_eliminate": "misleading positives",
    "meaning_of_misleading_positive": "An output that is coherent, useful, or persuasive at the practical layer while resting on a weak, incomplete, or invalid projection path at the structural layer."
  },
  "continuity_with_v14": {
    "preserve": [
      "signed field / signature state",
      "operator families and orientation handling",
      "corridor gating",
      "caution / hold / recovery",
      "trace salience and residue",
      "state export and regression discipline",
      "additive rollout behind flags or side paths"
    ],
    "do_not_preserve_as_center": [
      "readout-first success criteria",
      "implicit evaluation scattered across subsystems without a formal projection object"
    ],
    "non_regression_rule": "v14 remains executable baseline until v15 path matches or exceeds it on agreed checks."
  },
  "architectural_shift": {
    "v14_center": "projection -> stabilization -> readout",
    "v15_center": "structure -> admissibility -> projection -> readout",
    "explanation": "The system no longer asks whether an output can be produced; it asks whether a projection from full structure into usable signature is legitimate."
  },
